INNER JOIN [Category] AS [p.Category] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [p.Category].[Id]
ORDER BY [p].[DateCreated] DESC

INNER JOIN [Category] AS [p.Category] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [p.Category].[Id]
ORDER BY [p].[DateCreated] DESC, [p].[Id]

SELECT [p.Tags].[PostId], [p.Tags].[TagId], [p.Tag].[Id], [p.Tag].[DateCreated], [p.Tag].[DateLastUpdated], [p.Tag].[IsActive], [p.Tag].[Name]
FROM [PostTag] AS [p.Tags]
INNER JOIN [Tag] AS [p.Tag] ON [p.Tags].[TagId] = [p.Tag].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT DISTINCT [p0].[Id], [p0].[DateCreated]
    FROM [Post] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Category] AS [p.Category0] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [p.Category0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p.Tags].[PostId] = [t].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[DateCreated] DESC, [t].[Id]
